Women's Health Recommendations: Visit a Radiologist for a mammogram - you are aware of this and you know your next one needs to be in November 2022
Overview Notes: Vitamin D: your level is not very low but a level of 50 to 80 ng/ml is optimal. Supplement with vitamin D3 5000 iu daily and recheck level in 3 months. Once in optimal range reduce supplementation to 2000 iu daily.
Comment Key: ClinicalExamComment
Comment Value: None
Special Investigation Notes: Nil

Women's Health Recommendations: Visit a Radiologist for a mammogram - you are aware of this and you know your next one needs to be in November 2022
Overview Notes: Vitamin D: your level is not very low but a level of 50 to 80 ng/ml is optimal. Supplement with vitamin D3 5000 iu daily and recheck level in 3 months. Once in optimal range reduce supplementation to 2000 iu daily.
Comment Key: MensHealthRecommendation
Comment Value: None
Special Investigation Notes: Nil

Overview Notes: Vitamin D: your level is not very low but a level of 50 to 80 ng/ml is optimal. Supplement with vitamin D3 5000 iu daily and recheck level in 3 months. Once in optimal range reduce supplementation to 2000 iu daily.
Comment Key: VitalsRecommendation
Comment Value: None
Special Investigation Notes: Nil
